# Foreword
This Technical Report has been produced by the 3^rd^ Generation Partnership
Project (3GPP).
The contents of the present document are subject to continuing work within the
TSG and may change following formal TSG approval. Should the TSG modify the
contents of the present document, it will be re-released by the TSG with an
identifying change of release date and an increase in version number as
follows:
Version x.y.z
where:
x the first digit:
1 presented to TSG for information;
2 presented to TSG for approval;
3 or greater indicates TSG approved document under change control.
y the second digit is incremented for all changes of substance, i.e. technical
enhancements, corrections, updates, etc.
z the third digit is incremented when editorial only changes have been
incorporated in the document.
# 1 Scope
The present document is a technical report for Dual connectivity (DC) band
combinations of LTE xDL/1UL (x=1,2,3,4) + inter-band NR 2DL/1UL under Rel-15
time frame. The purpose is to gather the relevant background information and
studies in order to address Dual connectivity (DC) band combinations of LTE
xDL/1UL (x=1,2,3,4) + inter-band NR 2DL/1UL in Rel-15 as shown in Table 1-1.
Table 1-1: Release 15 DC band combination of LTE xDL/1UL (x=1,2,3,4) + inter-
band NR 2DL/1UL

reference to a 3GPP document (including a GSM document), a non-specific

# 3 Definitions, symbols and abbreviations
## 3.1 Definitions
For the purposes of the present document, the terms and definitions given in
TR 21.905 [1] and the following apply.\ A term defined in the present document
takes precedence over the definition of the same term, if any, in TR 21.905
[1].
## 3.2 Symbols
For the purposes of the present document, the following symbols apply:
ΔR~IB,c~ Allowed reference sensitivity relaxation due to support for inter-
band CA operation, for serving cell _c_.
ΔT~IB,c~ Allowed maximum configured output power relaxation due to support for
inter-band CA
F~DL_low~ The lowest frequency of the downlink operating band
F~DL_high~ The highest frequency of the downlink operating band
F~UL_low~ The lowest frequency of the uplink operating band
F~UL_high~ The highest frequency of the uplink operating band
## 3.3 Abbreviations
For the purposes of the present document, the abbreviations given in TR 21.905
[1] and the following apply.\ An abbreviation defined in the present document
takes precedence over the definition of the same abbreviation, if any, in TR
21.905 [1].
BS Base Station
CA Carrier Aggregation
CA_nX-nY Inter-band CA of component carrier(s) in one sub-block within Band X
and component carrier(s) in one sub-block within Band Y where X and Y are the
applicable NR operating band
CC Component Carriers
DL DownLink
FDD Frequency Division Duplex
IMD Inter-modulation
MSD Maximum Sensitivity Deduction
NR New RAT
SCS Subcarrier spacing
TDD Time Division Duplex
UE User Equipment
UL Up Link
# 4 Background
The present document is a technical report for Dual connectivity (DC) band
combinations of LTE xDL/1UL(x=1,2,3,4) + inter-band NR 2DL/1UL under Rel-15
time frame. It covers both the UE and BS side. The document is divided in two
different parts:
\- General part: this part covers BS and UE specific which is band combination
independent.
\- Specific band combination part: this part covers each band combination and
its specific issues independently from each other (i.e. one subclause is
defined per band combination)
The specific band combination parts are independent and therefore, the working
speed also differs.
## 4.1 TR Maintenance
A single company is responsible for introducing all approved TPs in the
current TR, i.e. TR editor. However, it is the responsibility of the contact
person of each band combination to ensure that the TPs related to the band
combination have been implemented.
# 5 DC band combination of LTE xDL/1UL(x=1,2,3,4) + inter-band NR 2DL/1UL:
General Part
## 5.1 UE RF architectures
Generally, RAN4 consider same example RF architecture which are described in
section 5.1 in TR37.863-01-01 [6].
To support multiple component carriers in LTE and NR, RAN4 consider specific
RF components such as Diplexer, Triplexer, Quadplexer and Hexaplexer to derive
self-interference problems according to the LTE NR DC band combinations.
## 5.2 Summary of self-interference studies
Table 5.2-1 summarizes the LTE NR DC band combinations with self-interference
problems for 3DL/2UL DC operation.

problems for 4DL/2UL DC operation.

|  | 60 |  | Yes | Yes | Yes |  |  |  |  |  |   
### 6.1.3 Co-existence studies
Co-existence studies and the protected bands for the lower order 2DL/2UL DC
configurations are already captured 37.863-01-01 [6]. For the additional 3rd
receive band, second order harmonic from Band n28 may fall into Band n75.
### 6.1.4 ∆T~IB~ and ∆R~IB~ values

below.

* * *

n28
* * *
### 6.1.5 MSD
The 2^nd^ harmonics of NR Band n28 is would interfered the reception of the NR
Band n75. To reduce the harmonic problem in n75 DL band, we consider harmonic
trap filter for this EN-DC_20A_n28A-n75A UE.
Table 6.1.5-1 is the common isolation assumption for the EN-DC_20A-n28A-n75A
UE FE components.
Table 6.1.5-1. EN-DC_20A_n28A-n75A UE RF FE component isolation parameters
* * *
                                Attenuation Value
B28 Tx in PA output 28 B28 PA H2 attenuation 35 B28 duplexer H2 attenuation 33
Harmonic filter 20 LB switch H2 120 Diplexer attenuation 25 Antenna isolation
0 Diplexer pathloss 0.7 MB switch attenuation 0.7 MB switch 130/110
(primary/secondary) nB75 Rx filter attenuation 1.5 nB75 Rx filter 110/110
(primary/secondary) B28 PA to n75 LNA isolation 60
* * *
The Table 6.1.5-2 is the common parameters for MSD analysis for EN-
DC_20A_n28A-n75A.
Table 6.1.5-2. EN-DC_20A_n28A-n75A UE RF FE component isolation parameters
* * *
Parameter Considering Harmonic Trap Filter  
Primary Diversity  
Value H2 level Value H2 level B28 Tx in PA output 28 28 B28 PA H2 attenuation
35 -7 35 -7 B28 duplexer H2 attenuation 33 -40 33 -40 Harmonic filter 20 -60
20 -60 LB switch H2 -120 -60.0 -120 -60.0 Diplexer attenuation 25 -85.0 25
-85.0 Antenna isolation 0 -85.0 10 -95.0 Diplexer pathloss 0.7 -85.7 0.7 -95.7
MB switch attenuation 0.7 -86.4 0.7 -96.4 MB switch -130 -86.4 -110 -96.2 nB75
Rx filter attenuation 1.5 -87.9 1.5 -97.7 nB75 Rx filter -110 -87.9 -110 -97.5
B28 PA to n75 LNA isolation 60 -67.0 60 -67.0 Composite **-66.96** **-66.99**
After MRC **28.1 dB**
* * *
From the Table 6.1.5-2, the required MSD levels for CA_n28A-n75A are derived
as below in Table 6.1.5-3.
Table 6.1.5-3. Estimated MSD level at NR Band n75
+-----------------------------------------------+---------+------+------+------+------+ | MSD due to 2^nd^ harmonic for the n75 DL band | | | | | | +-----------------------------------------------+---------+------+------+------+------+ | UL band | DL band | 5 | 10 | 15 | 20 | | | | | | | | | | | MHz | MHz | MHz | MHz | +-----------------------------------------------+---------+------+------+------+------+ | | | dB | dB | dB | dB | +-----------------------------------------------+---------+------+------+------+------+ | n28 | n75 | 28.1 | 25.3 | 24.0 | 22.8 | +-----------------------------------------------+---------+------+------+------+------+

### 6.6.3 Co-existence studies
Co-existence studies of Band 5 + Band n78 and Band 5+ Band n257 are already
captured in TR 37.863-01-01 [6]. Based on the table in TR 37.863-01-01 [6], we
can found that there were no self interference problem to 3rd own Rx bands.
### 6.6.4 ∆T~IB~ and ∆R~IB~ values

below.

* * *
Table 6.6.4-2: ΔR~IB~

Inter-band DC Configuration E-UTRA and NR Band ΔR~IB~ [dB] DC_5A_n78A-n257A 5
0.2 n78 0.5 n257 0
* * *
### 6.6.5 MSD
IMD issues are already analysed in TR 37.863-01-01 [6] and there is no IMD
issues to 3rd own Rx bands. Harmonics are expected in DC_5A_n78A-n257A
configuration. DC_5A_n78A has 7th and 8th harmonics from n78 into n257 but
there is no harmonic problems by 7th and 8th order between FR1 and FR2.
Furthermore, DC_5A_n257A has 4th harmonic from Band 5 into n78 but this
harmonic problem will be solved in DC_5A_n78A.

### 6.7.3 Co-existence studies
Co-existence studies of Band 7 + Band n78 and Band 7 + Band n257 are already
captured in TR 37.863-01-01 [6]. Based on the table in TR 37.863-01-01 [6], we
can found that there were no self interference problem to 3^rd^ own Rx bands.

### 6.7.5 MSD
No IMD issues are expected but harmonics are expected in DC_7A_n78A-n257A DC
configuration. DC_7A_n78A has 7th and 8th harmonics from n78 into n257 but
there is no harmonic problems by 7^th^ and 8^th^ order between FR1 and FR2.

### 6.8.3 UE co-existence studies
The harmonic and IMD products caused by DC_3A_n3A-n77A and protected bands
follow from those derived for the constituent fallback modes, DC_3A_n3A,
DC_3A_n77A, and CA_n3A-n77A. The co-existence studies of DC_3A_n3A and
DC_3A_n77A are already captured in TR 37.863-01-01 [6], and the co-existence
studies of CA_n3A-n77A are captured in TR 37.865-01-01. In rel-15, only Single
Tx Switched UL mode is supported for DC_3A_n3A.
\- The 2nd harmonic interference from Band 3 or Band n3 UL will fall into Band
n77 DL frequency range
\- Note that in Rel.15, only single tx switched UL mode is supported for
DC_3A_n3A.

0.2 n3 0.2 n77 0.5
* * *
### 6.8.5 MSD
IMD problems are already analysed in constituent low order combinations,
additional analysis is not needed.
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_3A_n3A: Harmonic problem already discussed
and solved in DC_3A_n77A, CA_n3A-n77A. Note that only Single Tx Switched UL
mode is supported for DC_3A_n3A in Rel.15.
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC _3A_n77A: Harmonic problem already discussed
and solved in DC_3A_n77A, CA_n3A-n77A. IMD problem already discussed and
solved in DC_3A_n77A.

### 6.12.3 Co-existence studies

follow from those derived for DC_20A_n78A. The summary of self-interference
issues are provided in TR 37.864-41-21, Table 5.2-1.

### 6.12.5 MSD
All MSD requirements for DC_20A_n76A-n78A are already covered by its fallback
modes. No additional MSD requirement is needed.

### 6.21.3 Co-existence studies
Based on co-existence studies of DC_1A-n78A and DC_1A_n79A specified in TR
37.863-01-01 [6], harmonics and IMD issues are identified as below.
Table 6.21.3-1: Co-existence studies of DC band combination of LTE 1DL/1UL +
inter-band NR 2DL/1UL
* * *
B1+n78+n79 DC_1A_n78A 3rd IMD into n79 3rd IMD problem will be FFS. If
consider synchronous TDD operation btw n78 and n79, MSD study is not
necessary. DC_1A_n79A 5th IMDs into n78 5th IMD problem will be FFS. If
consider synchronous TDD operation btw n78 and n79, MSD study is not
necessary.
* * *

### 6.26.3 Co-existence studies
Based on co-existence studies of DC_21A-n78A and DC_21A_n79A specified in TR
37.863-01-01 [6], harmonics and IMD issues are identified as below.
* * *
B21+n78+n79 DC_21A_n78A 2nd & 4th IMDs into n79 - These IMD problem are FFS.
If consider synchronous TDD operation btw n78 and n79, MSD study is not
necessary. DC_21A_n79A 2nd IMD into n78 - The IMD problem are FFS. If consider
synchronous TDD operation btw n78 and n79, MSD study is not necessary.
* * *

### 7.1.3 Co-existence studies
Co-existence studies of Band 1 + Band n78, Band 3 + Band n78, Band 1 + n257
and Band 3 + n257 are captured in TR 37.863-01-01 [6], own Rx impact of the
3rd band is the followings
\- 7th and 8th harmonics from n78 may fall into n257 and 2nd, 3rd and 5th
order IMD may fall into own Rx of Band 3 when dual uplink is configured with
Band 1 + Band n78
\- 7th and 8th harmonics from n78 may fall into n257 and 5th order IMD may
fall into own Rx of Band 1 when dual uplink is configured with Band 3 + Band
n78
\- 2nd harmonic from Band 1 may fall into n78 and 3rd order IMD may fall into
own Rx of Band 3 when dual uplink is configured with Band 1 + Band n257
\- 2nd harmonic from Band 3 may fall into n78 and 3rd order IMD may fall into
own Rx of Band 1 when dual uplink is configured with Band 3 + Band n257.
### 7.1.4 ∆T~IB~ and ∆R~IB~ values
For DC_1A-3A_n78A-n257A, the ∆T~IB,c~ and ∆R~IB~ values are given in the
tables below.
Table 7.1.4-1: ΔT~IB,c~
* * *
Inter-band DC Configuration E-UTRA and NR Band ΔT~IB,c~ [dB]
DC_1A-3A_n78A-n257A 1 0.6 3 0.6 n78 0.8 n257 0
* * *
Table 7.1.4-2: ΔR~IB~
* * *
Inter-band DC Configuration E-UTRA and NR Band ΔR~IB~ [dB] DC_1A-3A_n78A-n257A
1 0.2 3 0.2 n78 0.5 n257 0
* * *
### 7.1.5 MSD
IMD problems are already analysed in constituent low order combinations
between LTE bands and NR bands. 2DL/2UL and 3DL/2UL captured in 37.863-01-01
[6] and TR 37.863-02-01 [7] respectively and fallback modes are captured in
37.864-41-21. Therefore, additional analysis is not needed.
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_1A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be not
any impact to n257 and IMD issues on 3rd own Rx band will be covered in
DC_1A-3A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC _3A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be
not any impact to n257 and IMD problems will be covered in DC_1A-3A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_1A_n257A: Harmonic problem already discussed
and solved in DC_1A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_3A_n257A: Harmonic problem is already solved
in DC_3A_n78A

### 7.2.3 Co-existence studies
Co-existence studies of Band 1 + Band n78, Band 5 + Band n78, Band 1 + n257
and Band 5 + n257 are captured in TR 37.863-01-01 [6], own Rx impact of the
3rd band is the followings
\- 7th and 8th harmonics from n78 may fall into n257 and 5th order IMD may
fall into own Rx of Band 5 when dual uplink is configured with Band 1+ Band
n78
\- 7th and 8th harmonics from n78 may fall into n257 and 3rd order IMD may
fall into own Rx of Band 1 when dual uplink is configured with Band 5 + Band
n78
\- 2nd harmonic from Band 1 may fall into n78 when dual uplink is configured
with Band 1 + Band n257
\- 4th harmonic from Band 5 may fall into n78 when dual uplink is configured
with Band 5 + Band 257
### 7.2.4 ∆T~IB~ and ∆R~IB~ values

### 7.2.5 MSD
IMD problems are already analysed in constituent low order combinations
between LTE bands and NR bands. 2DL/2UL and 3DL/2UL captured in 37.863-01-01
[6] and TR 37.863-02-01 [7] respectively and fallback modes are captured in
37.864-41-21. Therefore, additional analysis is not needed.
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_1A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be not
any impact to n257 and 5th IMD problems is already covered in DC_1A-5A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_5A_n78A: There is no harmonic problems by 7th
& 8th order between FR1 and FR2 and 3rd order IMD problems is already covered
in DC_1A-5A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_1A_n257A: Harmonic problem is already
discussed and is solved in DC_1A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_5A_n257A: Harmonic problem is already solved
in DC_5A_n78A

\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_7A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be not
any impact to n257 and 4th IMD problem is already covered in DC_1A-7A_n78A

and is solved in DC_1A_n78A

### 7.5.3 Co-existence studies
Co-existence studies of Band 3 + Band n78, Band 7 + Band n78, Band 3 + n257
and Band 7 + n257 are captured in TR 37.863-01-01 [6]
\- 7th & 8th harmonics from n78 may fall into n257 when dual uplink is
configured with Band 3 + Band n78
\- 7th harmonic from Band 7 may fall into n257 and 3rd & 4th IMDs may fall
into Band 3 when dual uplink is configured with Band 7 + Band n78
\- 2nd harmonic from Band 3 may fall into n78 when dual uplink is configured
with Band 3 + Band n257

### 7.5.5 MSD
IMD problems are already analysed in constituent low order combinations
between LTE bands and NR bands. 2DL/2UL and 3DL/2UL captured in 37.863-01-01
[6] and TR 37.863-02-01 [7] respectively and fallback modes are captured in
37.864-41-21. Therefore, additional analysis is not needed.
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_3A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be not
any impact to n257
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_7A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be not
impact to n257 and IMD problems are already covered in DC_3A-7A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_3A_n257A: Harmonic problem is already solved
in DC_3A_n78A

Band 7 + Band n78

with Band 5 + Band n257

& 8th order between FR1 and FR2 and 2nd IMD problem is already covered in
DC_5A-7A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_7A_n78A: Up to 7th harmonic order will be not
any impact to n257 and IMD problems are already covered in DC_5A-7A_n78A
\- Uplink DC configuration is DC_5A_n257A: Harmonic problem is already solved
in DC_5A_n78A

37,864-41-21. Therefore, additional analysis is not needed.

### 9.5.3 Co-existence studies
The harmonic and IMD products caused by DC_1A-3A-7A-20A_n28A-n78A and
protected bands follow from those derived for the constituent fallback modes.
The summary of self-interference issues are provided in TR 37.864-41-21, Table
5.2-4.
### 9.5.4 ∆T~IB~ and ∆R~IB~ values
Same ∆T~IB,c~ and ∆R~IB~ values as DC_1A-3A-7A-20A-28A_n78A can be used as
shown in tables below.
Table 9.5.4-1: ΔT~IB,c~
* * *
Inter-band DC Configuration E-UTRA and NR Band ΔT~IB,c~ [dB]
DC_1A-3A-7A-20A_n28A-n78A 1 0.7 3 0.7 7 0.7 20 0.6 n28 0.6 n78 0.8
* * *
Table 9.5.4-2: ΔR~IB~
* * *
Inter-band DC Configuration E-UTRA and NR Band ΔR~IB~ [dB]
DC_1A-3A-7A-20A_n28A-n78A 1 0.2 3 0.2 7 0.2 20 0.2 n28 0.2 n78 0.5
* * *
### 9.5.5 MSD
All MSD requirements for DC_1A-3A-7A-20A_n28A-n78A are already covered by
constituent fallback modes. No additional MSD requirement is needed.
